2025-07-07 09:33:23 [DBG] Executing DbCommand [Parameters=[@__Trim_0='QI197B607BEA2C22C'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT q1."Id", q1."Category", q1."CreatedAt", q1."Description", q1."TimeLimit", q1."Title", q1."TotalMarks", q1."UploadedBy", s."Id", s."CreatedAt", s."Mark", s."QuestionText", s."QuizId", s."Id0", s."IsCorrect", s."OptionText", s."QuestionId"
FROM (
    SELECT q."Id", q."Category", q."CreatedAt", q."Description", q."TimeLimit", q."Title", q."TotalMarks", q."UploadedBy"
    FROM "Quizzes" AS q
    WHERE btrim(q."Id", E' \t\n\r') = @__Trim_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS q1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q0."Id", q0."CreatedAt", q0."Mark", q0."QuestionText", q0."QuizId", o."Id" AS "Id0", o."IsCorrect", o."OptionText", o."QuestionId"
    FROM "Questions" AS q0
    LEFT JOIN "Options" AS o ON q0."Id" = o."QuestionId"
) AS s ON q1."Id" = s."QuizId"
ORDER BY q1."Id", s."Id"

SELECT q1."Id", q1."Category", q1."CreatedAt", q1."Description", q1."TimeLimit", q1."Title", q1."TotalMarks", q1."UploadedBy", s."Id", s."CreatedAt", s."Mark", s."QuestionText", s."QuizId", s."Id0", s."IsCorrect", s."OptionText", s."QuestionId"
FROM (
    SELECT q."Id", q."Category", q."CreatedAt", q."Description", q."TimeLimit", q."Title", q."TotalMarks", q."UploadedBy"
    FROM "Quizzes" AS q
    WHERE btrim(q."Id", E' \t\n\r') = @__Trim_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS q1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q0."Id", q0."CreatedAt", q0."Mark", q0."QuestionText", q0."QuizId", o."Id" AS "Id0", o."IsCorrect", o."OptionText", o."QuestionId"
    FROM "Questions" AS q0
    LEFT JOIN "Options" AS o ON q0."Id" = o."QuestionId"
) AS s ON q1."Id" = s."QuizId"
ORDER BY q1."Id", s."Id"

SELECT q1."Id", q1."Category", q1."CreatedAt", q1."Description", q1."TimeLimit", q1."Title", q1."TotalMarks", q1."UploadedBy", s."Id", s."CreatedAt", s."Mark", s."QuestionText", s."QuizId", s."Id0", s."IsCorrect", s."OptionText", s."QuestionId"
FROM (
    SELECT q."Id", q."Category", q."CreatedAt", q."Description", q."TimeLimit", q."Title", q."TotalMarks", q."UploadedBy"
    FROM "Quizzes" AS q
    WHERE btrim(q."Id", E' \t\n\r') = @__Trim_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS q1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q0."Id", q0."CreatedAt", q0."Mark", q0."QuestionText", q0."QuizId", o."Id" AS "Id0", o."IsCorrect", o."OptionText", o."QuestionId"
    FROM "Questions" AS q0
    LEFT JOIN "Options" AS o ON q0."Id" = o."QuestionId"
) AS s ON q1."Id" = s."QuizId"
ORDER BY q1."Id", s."Id"
